 chimur loksabhaa seat kabhi congress kaa garh rahi he

 ) Mother Durga's motherhood is dedicated to Mother Skandamata

 They are also called as Mayuravahana, riding on Kumar, Shaktidhar and Mayur
 maa durga kaa yah naam shriskand (kartikeya) kii mata hone ke kaaran padaa
 Skanda Kumar sits in the lap of mother Skandamata as a child
 maa skandamata kii sawari singh hai evam bhujaaon main camel pushp hai
 Devotees who worship Maa Skanda Mata get happiness, peace and auspiciousness
 paanchaven navaratri ke vastron kaa rang evam prasad maa skandamata kii puja main aap shwet rang ke vastron kaa prayog kar sakate hai

 navaratri ke paanchaven din maa ko kele kaa naivaidhya chadhaane se aap sadaiv swasth rahenge
 On the fifth day of Navratri, the fifth power of Mother Durga is worshiped by Skandamata
 bhagwaan skanda kii mata hone hone ke kaaran maa durgaaki is paanchavin shakti ko skandamata ke naam se janaa jaataa he
 Lord Skanda is seated in the lap of mother in child form
 vahiin mata ne apni chaar bhujaaon main se dahini upari bhujaa ne bhagwaan skanda ko god main pakade hue hai
 It is believed that with the blessings of these children, along with the happiness of the children, they also get relief from sorrows
 navaratri main devi kii nau shaktiyon kii puja kii jaati he, lekin mul main teen deviyaan hi hai- mahakali, mahalakshmi or mahasaraswati
 These three goddesses are the power of the three Mahadevas
 navaratri main inhen teen shaktiyon kii alag-alag rup main puja kii jaati he

 lakshmi se hi vaibhav or yash miltaa he

 lakshmi chanchala he, vah ek jagah tik kar nahin rahati, isliye shastron kaa mat he ki inaki aradhana kabhi bhi akele nahin kerani chahie
 Worship him with Srinarayan
 devi ko ahankaar pasand nahin he
 Navami of Navratri is the day of Mahalakshmi
 is din inaki vishesh aradhana kerani chahie
 Worship of Skandamata on the fifth day of Navratri, worship Goddess with these mantras, Vidya is the second foundation of social honor
 gyaan, kala, sangeet, gunon se hi kisi vyakti kii samaaj main pahchaan hoti he
 He gets fame
 or isaki prapti ke liye maa saraswati kii aradhana jaruri he
 Lakshmi is unstable, fickle, but Saraswati ji is permanent, calm and unchanging
 saundarya va aarogy kii devi saubhaahgya or saundarya kii devi mukhyatyah parvati or mahalakshmi donon hai
